 ) The year is 1998
 tab mahesh gupta apni patni, bete or beti ke saath dilli ke south ekstansion jaisi posh colony main rahete the
 Despite being among the most expensive areas of Delhi, the people there were troubled by the supply of drinking water harmful to health
 mahesh ke bachche biimaar rahane lage
 He studied many of the "water purifiers" in the market but none were able to completely clean the "hard water" containing dirt
 ejeeniyar digridhari mahesh ne kaaphi research ke baad pataa lagaaya ki shriverse osmosisy (aaro) takneekee khaare pani kii ashuddhiyon ko dur karne main puri tarah kargar he
 What was then, Mahesh ordered all the equipment needed for RO technology from the US and in a few months made a "water purifier" with RO technology for his home use
 isane ghar main aane vaale khaare pani ko meetha bana diya
 Encouraged by the results, Mahesh now decided to make a foray into the field of manufacturing RO technical water purifiers
 yaheen se aaro takneekee vaale desh main bane pehle water purifaire kii neenv padi
 Kent RO Water Purifier, named after Kent, a county in southeastern England, came on the market
 bachapan se hi medhaavi rahe mahesh ne indian institute of technology (iity), kanpur se 1975 main mechanical ejineering kii degree hasil kii
 After this, he took a masters degree in petrochemicals from the Indian Institute of Petroleum for further studies
 padhai puri karne ke saath hi indian oil, mumbai main naukari kar lee
 Mahesh, who was aware of innovations from the beginning, did not like to work in a job tied
 indian oil main naukari ke dauraan mahesh ne tel ke kaarobaar ko baariki se dekha or unke man main hameshaa tel kii barabaadi ko rokane kii disha main kaam karne kaa khyaal kaundhta rahaa
 Eleven years later in 1988, Mahesh freed himself from his job
 unhone isi varsh noida main patni sunita or beti surabhi ke naam se ek company ''eses ejineering industries" banaai
 Through this company, Mahesh started manufacturing lubricating oil testing equipment and oil crillometers
 kuch hi dinon main eses ejineering oil flometre banane vaali desh kii sabase badi company ban gai
 However, Mahesh was recognized in the Indian market when he opened a factory in Sector-7, Noida in 1998 by forming a company named "kent RO System Limited"
 agle varsh 1999 main kent aaro ke naam se water purifaire bazaar main aa gaya
 Mahesh says, "in the year 1999, ordinary water purifiers cost Rs
 4-5,000
 main uplabdh tha lekin kent aaro kii keemat 20,000 ru
 was
 isliye shuruaati daur main reverse osmosis par aadhaarit water purifaire kharidne main logon ne zyada dilchaspee nahin dikhaai
 "alam was that in the first few years even five hundred pieces of Kent RO were not sold in a year
 isi dauraan 2003 main factory ko uttarakhand ke rudki sthanantarit kar diya gaya
 He started manufacturing the equipment used in water purifiers in his factory itself, which increased its quality and reliability
 kent aaro ke nirmaan ke chah varsh bitne ke baad varsh 2005 main mahesh ne apane khaas water purifaire kii branding karne kii baat sochi

 desh ke kai hisson main gende ke phool kii kheti kii jaati he

 babita ne 2010 dilli khelon main rajat or glasgo main 2014 main swarna padak jeeta tha
 Babitabita, who missed in the finals, looked weak in front of Diana's technique in the final
 dyna ne pehle hi bhartiya pahalwaan par dabaav banaate hue ek ank hasil kiye
 After this, Babita got two points by keeping her hold on Diana, but here the judges gave Diana two points and she again took a 3-2 lead
 babita ne mauka hasil karte hue dyna ke pair pakad unhen palatney kii koshish kii, lekin yahaan dyna ne daanv maarthe hue babita ko hi palatakar do or ank hasil kiye or ant main 5-2 se swarna padak apane naam kar liya or babita ko rajat padak se santosh karnaa padaa
 Babita's performance Babita performed brilliantly in the Commonwealth Games and went on to fight the opposing wrestlers in one game
 apane pehle mukaable main nigeria kii bose samual ko 2-1 se haraaya
 In the second match, Babita defeated Sri Lankan wrestler Deepika Dilhani 4–0
 tisare mukaable main babita ne australia kii karisa holland ko 4-0 se maat di
 But they had to face defeat in the final
 desh kii behtareen pahalwaan hai babitababita ne 2010 dilli kaamanwealth khelon main free style 51 kilogram main silver medal jeeta tha
 After this, he won the gold medal at the 2014 Glasgow Commonwealth Games
 babita asian championships (51kilogram) or world championships (55 kilogram) main desh ko bronj medal dilaa chuki hai
 Father Mahavir Phogat and star wrestler Sushil Kumar are Babita's role models and she draws inspiration from him
 gold coast main bhi susheel maujuudagi unhen nai urja di hogi
 Hafogat sisters have given a new identity to Indian women's wrestling
 mahavir phogot ne badi chunautiyan kaa saamana karte hue apni betiyon ko pahalwaan banaaya he
 Bollywood actor Aamir Khan's 'dangal' showed people how much Mahavir Singh Phogat struggled to make his daughters a wrestler
 bhaajapa ne aarope lagaaya ki kendriya mantri kamalnath or goa ke mukhyamantri digambar kaamat rajya ko prastaavit rashtriya rajmarg pariyojna ke liye bhoomi adhigrahan karne kii prakriya ke jariye lut rahe hai
 Leader of the Opposition in Goa Manohar Parrikar said that Kamal Nath, Chief Minister of Goa Kamat and the company were not following the model procedure in the matter of national highway extension
 unhone daawa kiya ki ve rashtriya rajmarg vistaar pariyojna ko rashtramandal khelon kii buniyadi sanrachana ke nirmaan main hue ghotaale kii tarah tabdeel kar rahe hai taaki rajya ko lutaa ja sake
 Congress President Sonia Gandhi could not travel to Uttarakhand to attend the rally
 bataaya jaataa he ki iskaa kaaran sonia gandhi kaa aswasth hona he
 Later, the written speech of Sonia Gandhi was read at the rally
 apane sandesh main sonia gandhi ne paroksh rup se team anna par nishaanaa saadhaa he
 In the message, without naming any member of Team Anna, Sonia Gandhi said that those who accuse others against corruption should also look within themselves
 sonia gandhi haal hi main videsh se surgery ke karaane ke baad lauti hai
 Congress general secretary Janardan Dwivedi said, 'sonia is currently suffering from fever
 unka uttrakhand daura sthagit kar diya gaya he
 Apart from addressing the rally, Sonia was also to lay the foundation stone of the rishikesh-karnprayag rail project at Gauchar in Chamoli district

 ritesh sidhvani or farhaan akhtar ne is film kaa nirmaan kiya he

 is film main ek kaalpanik desh he jiskaa naam he 'bangistan' jahaan do dharmon ke log apane phaayde ke liye videsh main ho rahe sarv dharm-sammelan main bam visphot karke duniya ko dahlaana chaahate hai

e
 Pulkit Samrat and Hafiz i
e

 Now the matter of strengths and shortcomings
 ye film maujuuda halaat par ek tanj he, jahaan aatankwaad se kai desh pareshaan hai or is mudde ko kamedi ke zariye film main dhaalane kii koshish kii gai he
 This sting of regret could not bring a smile to the face
 film dekhakar aap man hi man lekhak or nirdeshak ke ydia ko saraahte jarur hai, lekin film aapako na hansaa paati he or na rulaa paati he, yani kamazor script
 The comments pulakit ne kaaphi laud acting kii he, film ke kuch seens ghise-pite lage, masalan pulakit kii ramlila
 
 
 At the same time the warp knits of many scenes are well woven, but these prove to be ineffective
 vahiin film ke gaanon main bhi tanj he par ye jubaan par nahi chadhate
 Jacqueline had no work in the film, neither her character is effective nor her performance
 ab baat khoobiyon kii jisamen sabase pehle number aata he film kaa vishay, jo ki kamaal kaa he
 The way the story is pushed forward is also good, the film has a line - 'jab main tu bana and tu main, then we can understand each other', which is a very big thing in a nutshell
 ritesh apane kirdaar ke saath nyaay karte hai, film kaa screenple ksaa hua he
